You can now call Canada, Puerto Rico and the U.S. Virgin Islands!
Take your phone with you when you travel to Canada, Puerto Rico or the U.S. Virgin Islands.
AT&amp;T Wireless gives customers the capability to dial to and roam in these 3 areas. You'll use airtime just like a regular call, and pay for any additional airtime and roaming charges based on your current rate plan. Additional international long distance charges will apply to all calling to or from these areas. Other restrictions apply.
Visit attwireless.com/international for details.
